Refer to another app “LectureMate for Teachers’ for how to use lyrics files.\r\n\r\nAnother command is the Test signal. Before buying a Bluetooth controller you can use this command to test if a Bluetooth controller fits your needs. Most Bluetooth controllers simulate keyboard signals PgUp and PgDn, etc. The app supports keyboard key signals Left, Right, Up, Down, PgUp and PgDn, so you can, using the Test signal command, press these keys to see their functions in the app. For example, PgUp is used to Play or Pause playback, and PgDn is used to switch to the next music. Similarly, you test Bluetooth controller’s switches (pedals) to check if their functions may be used in this app.\r\n\r\nUse the Publisher link above or search “Gordon Huang” to find our other
